Performance of functions relating to financial market infrastructure

Section 56

##### New Chapter 2A of Part 18 of FSMA 2000

1

In Part 18 of FSMA 2000 (recognised investment exchanges, clearing houses and
CSDs), before Chapter 3B insert—

######### Performance of functions of recognised bodies

########## Relevant recognised bodies

########### Recognised bodies to which this Chapter applies

1.309A

1.309A.1

The Treasury may by regulations specify as a “ relevant recognised body ” for
the purposes of this Chapter a type of recognised body mentioned in subsection
(2) .

1.309A.2

The types of recognised bodies are—

1.309A.2.a

recognised investment exchanges;

1.309A.2.b

recognised central counterparties;

1.309A.2.c

recognised CSDs.

1.309A.3

Before making regulations under subsection  (1) , the Treasury—

1.309A.3.a

must consult the FCA if it proposes to specify recognised investment exchanges
(or recognised investment exchanges of a specified description);

1.309A.3.b

must consult the Bank of England if it proposes to specify recognised central
counterparties or recognised CSDs (or recognised central counterparties or
recognised CSDs of a specified description);

1.309A.3.c

in any case, must consult such persons as appear to it to be representative of
interests likely to be affected by the application of this Chapter to the
types, or descriptions, of bodies it proposes to specify.

1.309A.4

In this Chapter, references to “the appropriate regulator” are to be read in
accordance with section 285A (accordingly, the appropriate regulator in
relation to a recognised investment exchange is the FCA, and in any other case
is the Bank of England).

1.309A.5

Nothing in this Chapter applies to overseas investment exchanges.

########## Prohibition

########### Part 18 prohibition orders

1.309B

1.309B.1

This section applies if it appears to the appropriate regulator that an
individual is not a fit and proper person to perform functions in relation to
an activity carried on by a relevant recognised body.

1.309B.2

The appropriate regulator may make an order (a “Part 18 prohibition order”)
prohibiting the individual from performing a specified function, any function
falling within a specified description or any function.

1.309B.3

A Part 18 prohibition order may relate to—

1.309B.3.a

a specified activity, any activity falling within a specified description or
all activities (but see subsection  (5) );

1.309B.3.b

all persons falling within subsection  (4) , or a particular paragraph of that
subsection, or all persons within a specified class of person falling within a
particular paragraph of that subsection.

1.309B.4

A person falls within this subsection if the person is—

1.309B.4.a

a relevant recognised body (whether or not the appropriate regulator making
the order is the appropriate regulator in relation to relevant recognised
bodies of that type),

1.309B.4.b

an authorised person,

1.309B.4.c

an exempt person (other than a relevant recognised body), or

1.309B.4.d

a person to whom, as a result of Part 20, the general prohibition does not
apply in relation to a regulated activity.

1.309B.5

If a Part 18 prohibition order makes provision in relation to a person or
persons falling within subsection  (4) (b) ,  (c)  or  (d) , subsection
(3)(a)  applies in relation to such provision as if references to an activity
or activities were to a regulated activity or regulated activities.

1.309B.6

In this section, “ specified ” means specified in the Part 18 prohibition
order.

########### Procedure for making Part 18 prohibition orders

1.309C

1.309C.1

If the appropriate regulator proposes to make a Part 18 prohibition order it
must—

1.309C.1.a

comply with such consultation requirements as may be prescribed, and

1.309C.1.b

give the individual to whom the order would apply a warning notice.

1.309C.2

A warning notice under subsection  (1)(b)  must set out the terms of the
prohibition.

1.309C.3

If the appropriate regulator decides to make a Part 18 prohibition order it
must give the individual to whom the order applies a decision notice.

1.309C.4

The decision notice must—

1.309C.4.a

name the individual to whom the Part 18 prohibition order applies, and

1.309C.4.b

set out the terms of the order.

1.309C.5

If the appropriate regulator decides to make a Part 18 prohibition order, the
individual to whom the order applies may refer the matter to the Tribunal.

########### Varying and withdrawing Part 18 prohibition orders

1.309D

1.309D.1

This section applies where the appropriate regulator has made a Part 18
prohibition order in relation to an individual.

1.309D.2

The appropriate regulator may vary or revoke the Part 18 prohibition order on
the application of the individual.

1.309D.3

Before varying or revoking a Part 18 prohibition order, the appropriate
regulator must comply with such consultation requirements as may be
prescribed.

1.309D.4

On an application for the variation or revocation of a Part 18 prohibition
order—

1.309D.4.a

if the appropriate regulator decides to grant the application, it must give
the applicant written notice of its decision;

1.309D.4.b

if the appropriate regulator proposes to refuse the application, it must give
the applicant a warning notice;

1.309D.4.c

if the appropriate regulator decides to refuse the application, it must give
the applicant a decision notice.

1.309D.5

If the appropriate regulator gives the applicant a decision notice under
subsection  (4)(c) , the applicant may refer the matter to the Tribunal.

########### Offence of breaching prohibition

1.309E

1.309E.1

An individual who performs a function, or agrees to perform a function, in
breach of a Part 18 prohibition order is guilty of an offence.

1.309E.2

An individual who commits an offence under this section is liable—

1.309E.2.a

on summary conviction in England and Wales, to a fine;

1.309E.2.b

on summary conviction in Scotland, to a fine not exceeding level 5 on the
standard scale;

1.309E.2.c

on summary conviction in Northern Ireland, to a fine not exceeding level 5 on
the standard scale.

1.309E.3

In proceedings for an offence under this section, it is a defence for the
individual to show that the individual took all reasonable precautions and
exercised all due diligence to avoid committing the offence.

########### Duty in relation to prohibited individuals

1.309F

1.309F.1

A person (“ P ”) falling within section  309B (4)  must take reasonable care
to ensure that no function in relation to the carrying on of P’s activities is
performed by an individual who is prohibited from performing that function by
a Part 18 prohibition order.

1.309F.2

A contravention of subsection  (1)  is actionable at the suit of a private
person who suffers loss as a result of the contravention, subject to the
defences and other incidents applying to actions for breach of statutory duty.

1.309F.3

In prescribed cases, a contravention of subsection  (1)  which would be
actionable at the suit of a private person is actionable at the suit of a
person who is not a private person, subject to the defences and other
incidents applying to actions for breach of statutory duty.

1.309F.4

In this section “private person” has such meaning as may be prescribed.

########## Approval

########### Requirement for approval

1.309G

1.309G.1

A relevant recognised body must take reasonable care to ensure that a person
does not perform a designated senior management function in relation to the
carrying on of an activity by the body, unless the person is acting in
accordance with an approval given by the appropriate regulator under this
section.

1.309G.2

Subsection  (1)  applies only in relation to a function performed under—

1.309G.2.a

an arrangement entered into by the relevant recognised body, or

1.309G.2.b

an arrangement entered into by a contractor of the relevant recognised body.

1.309G.3

“ Designated senior management function ” means a function of a description
specified in rules made by the appropriate regulator.

1.309G.4

The appropriate regulator may specify a description of function under
subsection  (3)  only if it is satisfied that the function is a senior
management function.

1.309G.5

A function is a “ senior management function ” in relation to the carrying on
of a relevant recognised body’s activities if—

1.309G.5.a

the function will require the person performing it to be responsible for
managing one or more aspects of the body’s affairs, and

1.309G.5.b

those aspects involve, or might involve, a risk of serious consequences—

1.309G.5.b.i

for the body, or

1.309G.5.b.ii

for business or other interests in the United Kingdom.

1.309G.6

In subsection  (5)(a) , the reference to managing one or more aspects of a
relevant recognised body’s affairs includes a reference to taking decisions,
or participating in the taking of decisions, about how one or more aspects of
those affairs should be carried on.

1.309G.7

In subsection  (2) , “arrangement”—

1.309G.7.a

means any kind of arrangement for the performance of a function of a relevant
recognised body which is entered into by the body, or by a contractor of the
body, and another person, and

1.309G.7.b

includes, in particular, an arrangement under which the other person is
appointed to an office, becomes a partner or is employed (whether under a
contract of service or otherwise).

########### Rules under section 

1.309H

1.309H.1

In relation to rules made by the Bank of England or the FCA under section
309G (3) , the power conferred by section 137T(c) to make transitional
provision includes, in particular, power—

1.309H.1.a

to provide for anything done under this Chapter, or under Part 5 (performance
of regulated activities), in relation to a senior management function of a
particular description to be treated as having been done in relation to a
senior management function of a different description;

1.309H.1.b

to provide for anything done under this Chapter, or under Part 5 (including
any application or order made, any requirement imposed and any approval or
notice given) to cease to have effect, to continue to have effect, or to
continue to have effect with modifications, or subject to time limits or
conditions;

1.309H.1.c

to provide for rules made by the regulator making the rules under section
309G (3)  to apply with modifications;

1.309H.1.d

to make saving provision.

1.309H.2

The Treasury may by regulations make whatever incidental, consequential,
transitional, supplemental or saving provision the Treasury consider
appropriate in connection with the making of rules under section  309G (3) .

1.309H.3

Regulations under subsection  (2)  may—

1.309H.3.a

confer functions on the Bank of England or the FCA (including the function of
making rules);

1.309H.3.b

modify legislation (including any provision of, or made under, this Act).

1.309H.4

In subsection  (3)(b) —

“ legislation ” means primary legislation, subordinate legislation (within the
meaning of the Interpretation Act 1978) and retained direct EU legislation,
but does not include rules or other instruments made by any regulator; “
modify ” includes amend, repeal or revoke.

########### Applications for approval

1.309I

1.309I.1

A relevant recognised body may apply for approval from the appropriate
regulator under section  309G  for a person to perform a designated senior
management function in relation to the carrying on of the body’s activities.

1.309I.2

The application must be made in such manner as the appropriate regulator may
direct.

1.309I.3

The application must contain—

1.309I.3.a

a statement setting out the aspects of the applicant’s affairs which it is
intended that the person will be responsible for managing in performing the
function, and

1.309I.3.b

such other information as the appropriate regulator may reasonably require.

1.309I.4

A statement provided under subsection  (3)(a)  is known as a “statement of
responsibilities”.

1.309I.5

At any time after the application is received, and before it is determined,
the appropriate regulator may require the applicant to provide it with such
further information as it reasonably considers necessary to enable it to
determine the application.

1.309I.6

The appropriate regulator may require the applicant to present information
provided under this section in such form, or to verify the information in such
a way, as the appropriate regulator may direct.

1.309I.7

Different directions may be given, and different requirements may be imposed,
in relation to different applications or categories of application.

1.309I.8

In subsection  (1) , “ relevant recognised body ” includes—

1.309I.8.a

if recognised investment exchanges are a type of recognised body to which this
Chapter applies, a person who has applied for recognition as such under
section 287;

1.309I.8.b

if recognised central counterparties are a type of recognised body to which
this Chapter applies, a person who has applied for recognition as such under
section 288;

1.309I.8.c

if recognised CSDs are a type of recognised body to which this Chapter
applies, a person who has applied for recognition as such under section 288A.

########### Vetting by relevant recognised bodies

1.309J

1.309J.1

Before making an application under section  309I  for approval for a person to
perform a designated senior management function, a relevant recognised body
must be satisfied that the person is a fit and proper person to perform the
function.

1.309J.2

In deciding that question, the relevant recognised body must have regard,
among other things, to whether the person, or any person who may perform a
function on the person’s behalf—

1.309J.2.a

has obtained a specified qualification;

1.309J.2.b

has undergone, or is undergoing, specified training;

1.309J.2.c

possesses a specified level of competence;

1.309J.2.d

has specified personal characteristics.

1.309J.3

In subsection  (2) , “ specified ” means specified in rules made by the
appropriate regulator.

1.309J.4

Before making rules for the purposes of this section, the appropriate
regulator must comply with such consultation requirements as may be
prescribed.

########### Determining applications: power to grant approval

1.309K

1.309K.1

The appropriate regulator may grant an application under section  309I  for
approval for a person to perform a designated senior management function only
if—

1.309K.1.a

it is satisfied that the person is a fit and proper person to perform the
function, or

1.309K.1.b

it is satisfied that the condition in paragraph  (a)  will be met if the
application is granted subject to one or more conditions (see subsection  (3)
).

1.309K.2

In determining the application, the appropriate regulator may have regard,
among other things, to the matters mentioned in section  309J (2)
(qualifications etc of person for whom approval sought).

1.309K.3

The appropriate regulator may, if it appears to it that it is desirable to do
so in order to advance a relevant objective—

1.309K.3.a

grant the application subject to any conditions that it considers appropriate;

1.309K.3.b

grant the application so as to give approval only for a limited period.

1.309K.4

For the purposes of subsection  (3) , “ relevant objective ” means—

1.309K.4.a

if the appropriate regulator is the FCA, any of its operational objectives;

1.309K.4.b

if the appropriate regulator is the Bank of England, the Financial Stability
Objective.

1.309K.5

Before granting approval under this section (whether or not subject to
conditions or for a limited period), the appropriate regulator must comply
with such consultation requirements as may be prescribed.

########### Determining applications: period for approval

1.309L

1.309L.1

The appropriate regulator must, before the end of the period for
consideration, determine whether—

1.309L.1.a

to grant an application under section  309I  for approval for a person to
perform a function, without imposing conditions or limiting the period for
which the approval has effect, or

1.309L.1.b

to give a warning notice under section  309M (2) .

1.309L.2

In subsection  (1) , “ the period for consideration ” means the period of 3
months beginning with the day on which the appropriate regulator receives the
application.

This is subject to subsections  (3)  and  (4) .

1.309L.3

Where the application under section  309I  is made by a person in reliance on
section  309I (8)  (applicants for recognition to be treated as relevant
recognised bodies), “ the period for consideration ” means whichever of the
following periods ends later—

1.309L.3.a

the period described in subsection  (2) , and

1.309L.3.b

the period within which the person’s application for recognition must be
determined—

1.309L.3.b.i

in the case of an application under section 287, in accordance with section
290(1B);

1.309L.3.b.ii

in the case of an application under section 288, in accordance with Article
17(7) of the EMIR regulation;

1.309L.3.b.iii

in the case of an application under section 288A, in accordance with section
290(4A).

1.309L.4

If the appropriate regulator imposes a requirement under section  309I (5) ,
the period described in subsection  (2)  stops running on the day on which the
requirement is imposed but starts running again—

1.309L.4.a

on the day on which the required information is received by the appropriate
regulator, or

1.309L.4.b

if the information is not provided on a single day, on the last of the days on
which it is received by the appropriate regulator.

1.309L.5

An applicant may withdraw an application under section  309I , by giving
written notice to the appropriate regulator, at any time before the
appropriate regulator determines the application, but only with the consent
of—

1.309L.5.a

the person in relation to whom the application is made, and

1.309L.5.b

the person by whom that person is to be retained to perform the function to
which the application relates, if not the applicant.

########### Determining applications: further procedure

1.309M

1.309M.1

If the appropriate regulator decides to grant an application under section
309I  without imposing conditions or limiting the period for which approval is
given, it must give written notice of its decision to each of the interested
parties.

1.309M.2

If the appropriate regulator proposes to refuse the application, or to grant
the application subject to conditions or for a limited period (or both), it
must give a warning notice to each of the interested parties.

1.309M.3

If the appropriate regulator decides to refuse the application, or to grant
the application subject to conditions or for a limited period (or both), it
must give a decision notice to each of the interested parties.

1.309M.4

If the appropriate regulator decides to refuse the application, or to grant
the application subject to conditions or for a limited period (or both), each
of the interested parties may refer the matter to the Tribunal.

1.309M.5

In this section, “ the interested parties ”, in relation to an application
under section  309I  for approval for a person to perform a function, are—

1.309M.5.a

the applicant,

1.309M.5.b

the person in relation to whom the application is made, and

1.309M.5.c

the person by whom that person is to be retained to perform the function to
which the application relates, if not the applicant.

########### Changes in responsibilities

1.309N

1.309N.1

This section applies where, on an application made by a relevant recognised
body under section  309I , the appropriate regulator has given approval for a
person to perform a designated senior management function (and has not
withdrawn the approval).

1.309N.2

Each time there is a notifiable change in the aspects of the relevant
recognised body’s affairs which the person is responsible for managing in
performing the function, the relevant recognised body must provide the
appropriate regulator with a revised statement of responsibilities (see
section  309I (4) ).

1.309N.3

Whether a change is “notifiable” is to be determined by the relevant
recognised body in accordance with rules made by the appropriate regulator.

1.309N.4

The appropriate regulator may require the relevant recognised body to present
information provided under this section in such form, or to verify the
information in such a way, as the appropriate regulator may direct.

########### Withdrawing approval

1.309O

1.309O.1

This section applies if an approval under section 309G has been given by the
appropriate regulator in relation to the performance by a person of a
designated senior management function.

1.309O.2

The appropriate regulator may withdraw the approval if it considers that the
person is not a fit and proper person to perform the function.

1.309O.3

In considering whether to withdraw an approval, the appropriate regulator may
take into account any matter which may be taken into account in considering an
application under section  309I .

1.309O.4

The relevant recognised body on whose application the approval was given must,
at specified intervals—

1.309O.4.a

consider whether there are grounds on which the appropriate regulator could
withdraw the approval under this section, and

1.309O.4.b

if it considers that there are such grounds, notify the appropriate regulator
of those grounds.

1.309O.5

For the purposes of subsection  (4) , a “specified interval” is an interval
specified in rules made by the appropriate regulator for the purposes of this
section.

########### Procedure for withdrawing approval

1.309P

1.309P.1

If the appropriate regulator proposes to withdraw an approval given under
section  309G , it must—

1.309P.1.a

comply with such consultation requirements as may be prescribed, and

1.309P.1.b

give each of the interested parties a warning notice.

1.309P.2

If the appropriate regulator decides to withdraw the approval, it must give
each of the interested parties a decision notice.

1.309P.3

If the appropriate regulator decides to withdraw the approval, each of the
interested parties may refer the matter to the Tribunal.

1.309P.4

In this section, “ the interested parties ”, in relation to an approval given
under section  309G , are—

1.309P.4.a

the relevant recognised body on whose application the approval was given,

1.309P.4.b

the person in relation to whom the approval was given, and

1.309P.4.c

the person by whom that person’s services are retained, if not the relevant
recognised body.

########### Varying approval at request of relevant recognised body

1.309Q

1.309Q.1

Where an approval under section  309G  has effect subject to conditions, the
relevant recognised body that applied for the approval may apply to the
appropriate regulator to vary the approval by—

1.309Q.1.a

varying a condition,

1.309Q.1.b

removing a condition, or

1.309Q.1.c

imposing a new condition.

1.309Q.2

Where an approval under section  309G  has effect for a limited period, the
relevant recognised body that applied for the approval may apply to the
appropriate regulator to vary the approval by—

1.309Q.2.a

varying the period, or

1.309Q.2.b

removing the limit on the period for which the approval is to have effect.

1.309Q.3

The appropriate regulator must, before the end of the consultation period,
determine whether—

1.309Q.3.a

to grant the application, or

1.309Q.3.b

to give a warning notice under section  309M (2)  (as applied by subsection
(8) ).

1.309Q.4

The “consultation period” is—

1.309Q.4.a

such period as may be prescribed (and different periods may be prescribed in
relation to different types of relevant recognised bodies), or

1.309Q.4.b

if no such period is prescribed, the period of 3 months beginning with the day
on which the appropriate regulator receives the application to vary the
approval.

1.309Q.5

The appropriate regulator may refuse an application under this section, if it
appears to it that it is desirable to do so in order to advance a relevant
objective.

1.309Q.6

For the purposes of subsection  (5) , “ relevant objective ” means—

1.309Q.6.a

if the appropriate regulator is the FCA, any of its operational objectives;

1.309Q.6.b

if the appropriate regulator is the Bank of England, the Financial Stability
Objective.

1.309Q.7

An application may not be made under this section to vary or remove a
condition or limit that was imposed under section  309Z2 .

1.309Q.8

Except as provided for below, the following sections apply to an application
under this section for variation of an approval as they apply to an
application under section  309I —

1.309Q.8.a

section  309I (2)  to  (8) ,

1.309Q.8.b

section  309L (4)  and  (5) , and

1.309Q.8.c

section  309M , but as if the references in subsections  (1)  to  (4)  to
granting the application subject to conditions or for a limited period, or
without imposing conditions or limiting the period for which approval is
given, were omitted.

########### Varying approval on the appropriate regulator’s initiative

1.309R

1.309R.1

The appropriate regulator may vary an approval under section  309G  if it
considers it desirable to do so in order to advance a relevant objective.

1.309R.2

For these purposes, “ relevant objective ” means—

1.309R.2.a

if the appropriate regulator is the FCA, any of its operational objectives;

1.309R.2.b

if the appropriate regulator is the Bank of England, the Financial Stability
Objective.

1.309R.3

The appropriate regulator may vary the approval by doing the following—

1.309R.3.a

imposing a condition,

1.309R.3.b

varying a condition,

1.309R.3.c

removing a condition,

1.309R.3.d

where the approval has effect for an unlimited period, limiting the period of
the approval, or

1.309R.3.e

where the approval has effect for a limited period, varying that period or
removing the limit on the period.

1.309R.4

A variation under this section takes effect—

1.309R.4.a

immediately, if the notice given under subsection  (5)  states that to be the
case,

1.309R.4.b

on a date specified in the notice, or

1.309R.4.c

if no date is specified in the notice, when the matter to which the notice
relates is no longer open to review.

1.309R.5

If the appropriate regulator proposes to vary an approval or varies an
approval with immediate effect, it must give each of the interested parties
written notice—

1.309R.5.a

setting out details of the variation,

1.309R.5.b

stating the reasons for the variation,

1.309R.5.c

stating that each of the interested parties may make representations to the
appropriate regulator within the period specified in the notice (whether or
not any of the interested parties has referred the matter to the Tribunal),

1.309R.5.d

stating when the variation takes effect, and

1.309R.5.e

setting out each interested party’s right to refer the matter to the Tribunal.

1.309R.6

A variation may be expressed to take effect immediately or on a specified date
only if the appropriate regulator, having regard to its reason for varying the
approval, reasonably considers that it is necessary for the variation to take
effect immediately or on that date (as appropriate).

1.309R.7

The appropriate regulator may extend the period allowed under the notice for
making representations.

1.309R.8

The appropriate regulator must give each of the interested parties written
notice if, having considered the representations made, it decides—

1.309R.8.a

to vary the approval, or

1.309R.8.b

if the variation has taken effect, not to rescind it.

1.309R.9

A notice under subsection  (8)  must inform the interested parties of the
right of each of them to refer the matter to the Tribunal.

1.309R.10

The appropriate regulator must give each of the interested parties written
notice if, having considered the representations made, it decides—

1.309R.10.a

not to vary the approval,

1.309R.10.b

to vary the approval in a different way, or

1.309R.10.c

if the variation has taken effect, to rescind it.

1.309R.11

A notice under subsection  (10)(b)  must comply with the requirements set out
in subsection  (5)(a)  to  (e) .

1.309R.12

A notice under this section which informs the interested parties of the right
to refer a matter to the Tribunal must give an indication of the procedure on
such a reference.

1.309R.13

In this section, “ the interested parties ” has the same meaning as in section
309P .

1.309R.14

For the purposes of subsection  (4)(c) , whether a matter is open to review is
to be determined in accordance with section 391(8).

########### Statement of policy on approval

1.309S

1.309S.1

The appropriate regulator must prepare and issue a statement of its policy
with respect to—

1.309S.1.a

the giving of approval under section  309G  subject to conditions or for a
limited period only, and

1.309S.1.b

the variation under section  309Q  or  309R  of an approval given under
section  309G .

1.309S.2

The appropriate regulator—

1.309S.2.a

may alter or replace a statement issued under this section, and

1.309S.2.b

if it does so, must issue the altered or replacement statement.

1.309S.3

Before the appropriate regulator issues a statement of policy under this
section, it must publish a draft of the proposed statement in the way
appearing to it to be best calculated to bring it to the attention of the
public.

1.309S.4

The draft statement must be accompanied by a notice stating that
representations about the proposal may be made to the appropriate regulator
within a period specified in the notice.

1.309S.5

Before issuing the proposed statement, the appropriate regulator must have
regard to any representations made to it in accordance with subsection  (4) .

1.309S.6

If the appropriate regulator issues the proposed statement it must publish the
following in the way appearing to it to be best calculated to bring them to
the attention of the public—

1.309S.6.a

the statement,

1.309S.6.b

an account, in general terms, of the representations made to it in accordance
with subsection  (4)  and its response to them, and

1.309S.6.c

if the statement issued differs from the draft published under subsection  (3)
in a way which the appropriate regulator considers to be significant, details
of the difference.

1.309S.7

The appropriate regulator may charge a reasonable fee for providing a person
with—

1.309S.7.a

a copy of a draft statement published under subsection  (3) , or

1.309S.7.b

a copy of a statement published under subsection  (6)(a) .

1.309S.8

The appropriate regulator must, without delay, give the Treasury a copy of
each statement it publishes under subsection  (6)(a) .

########### Breach of statutory duty by relevant recognised bodies

1.309T

1.309T.1

A contravention of section  309G (1) is actionable at the suit of a private
person who suffers loss as a result of the contravention, subject to the
defences and other incidents applying to actions for breach of statutory duty.

1.309T.2

In prescribed cases, a contravention of section  309G (1) which would be
actionable at the suit of a private person is actionable at the suit of a
person who is not a private person, subject to the defences and other
incidents applying to actions for breach of statutory duty.

1.309T.3

In this section “private person” has such meaning as may be prescribed.

########### Power to impose penalties

1.309U

1.309U.1

The appropriate regulator may impose a penalty on a person if it is satisfied
that—

1.309U.1.a

the person has at any time performed a designated senior management function
without approval, and

1.309U.1.b

at that time the person knew, or could reasonably be expected to have known,
that they were performing a designated senior management function without
approval.

1.309U.2

The penalty may be of such amount as the appropriate regulator considers
appropriate.

1.309U.3

A person performs a designated senior management function without approval at
a time if—

1.309U.3.a

the person performs a designated senior management function under an
arrangement entered into by a relevant recognised body, or by a contractor of
a relevant recognised body, in relation to the carrying on of an activity by
the body, and

1.309U.3.b

when performing the function, the person is not acting in accordance with an
approval given under section  309G .

1.309U.4

The appropriate regulator may not impose a penalty on a person under this
section after the end of the limitation period unless it gave the person a
warning notice under section  309V  before the end of that period.

1.309U.5

For the purposes of subsection  (4) —

1.309U.5.a

“ the limitation period ” means the period of 6 years beginning with the first
day on which the appropriate regulator knew that the person concerned had
performed a designated senior management function without approval, and

1.309U.5.b

the appropriate regulator is to be treated as knowing that a person has
performed a designated senior management function without approval if it has
information from which that can reasonably be inferred.

########### Procedure for imposing penalties

1.309V

1.309V.1

If the appropriate regulator proposes to impose a penalty on a person under
section  309U , it must give the person a warning notice.

1.309V.2

A warning notice under this section must state the amount of the penalty.

1.309V.3

If the appropriate regulator decides to impose a penalty on a person under
section  309U , it must give the person a decision notice.

1.309V.4

A decision notice under this section must state the amount of the penalty.

1.309V.5

If the appropriate regulator decides to impose a penalty on a person under
section  309U , the person may refer the matter to the Tribunal.

########### Statement of policy on penalties

1.309W

1.309W.1

The appropriate regulator must prepare and issue a statement of its policy
with respect to—

1.309W.1.a

the imposition of penalties under section  309U , and

1.309W.1.b

the amount of penalties under that section.

1.309W.2

The appropriate regulator’s policy in determining whether a penalty should be
imposed, and what the amount of a penalty should be, must include having
regard to—

1.309W.2.a

the conduct of the person on whom the penalty is to be imposed,

1.309W.2.b

the extent to which the person could reasonably be expected to have known that
a designated senior management function was performed without approval,

1.309W.2.c

the length of the period during which the person performed a designated senior
management function without approval, and

1.309W.2.d

whether the person on whom the penalty is to be imposed is an individual.

1.309W.3

The appropriate regulator’s policy in determining whether a penalty should be
imposed on a person must also include having regard to the appropriateness of
taking action against the person instead of, or in addition to, taking action
against a relevant recognised body.

1.309W.4

A statement issued under this section must include an indication of the
circumstances in which the appropriate regulator would expect to be satisfied
that a person could reasonably be expected to have known that the person was
performing a designated senior management function without approval.

1.309W.5

The appropriate regulator—

1.309W.5.a

may alter or replace a statement issued under this section, and

1.309W.5.b

if it does so, must issue the altered or replacement statement.

1.309W.6

When imposing, or deciding whether to impose, a penalty on a person under
section  309U , the appropriate regulator must have regard to any statement of
policy published under this section (which was in force at a time when the
person performed a designated senior management function without approval).

########### Procedure for statement of policy on penalties

1.309X

1.309X.1

Before the appropriate regulator issues a statement under section  309W (1)
or  (5) , it must publish a draft of the proposed statement in the way
appearing to it to be best calculated to bring it to the attention of the
public.

1.309X.2

The draft statement must be accompanied by a notice stating that
representations about the proposal may be made to the appropriate regulator
within the period specified in the notice.

1.309X.3

Before issuing the proposed statement, the appropriate regulator must have
regard to any representations made to it in accordance with subsection  (2) .

1.309X.4

If the appropriate regulator issues the proposed statement it must publish the
following in the way appearing to it to be best calculated to bring them to
the attention of the public—

1.309X.4.a

the statement,

1.309X.4.b

an account, in general terms, of the representations made to the appropriate
regulator in accordance with subsection  (2)  and the appropriate regulator’s
response to them, and

1.309X.4.c

if the statement issued differs from the draft published under subsection  (1)
in a way which the appropriate regulator considers to be significant, details
of the difference.

1.309X.5

The appropriate regulator may charge a reasonable fee for providing a person
with—

1.309X.5.a

a copy of a draft statement published under subsection  (1) , or

1.309X.5.b

a copy of a statement published under subsection  (4)(a) .

1.309X.6

The appropriate regulator must, without delay, give the Treasury a copy of a
statement which it publishes under subsection  (4)(a) .

########## Certification of employees

########### Certification of employees by relevant recognised bodies

1.309Y

1.309Y.1

A relevant recognised body must take reasonable care to ensure that none of
its employees performs a specified function in relation to the carrying on of
an activity by the body, unless the employee has a valid certificate issued by
the body under section  309Z .

1.309Y.2

Subsection  (1)  applies only in relation to a function performed under an
arrangement entered into by the body.

1.309Y.3

In this section, “ specified function ” means a function of a description
specified in rules made by the appropriate regulator.

1.309Y.4

The appropriate regulator may specify a description of function under
subsection  (3)  only if, in relation to the carrying on of an activity by a
relevant recognised body of a particular description—

1.309Y.4.a

the function is not a designated senior management function in relation to the
carrying on of that activity by a relevant recognised body of that
description, and

1.309Y.4.b

the appropriate regulator is satisfied that the function is a significant-harm
function.

1.309Y.5

A function is a “ significant-harm function ”, in relation to the carrying on
of an activity by a relevant recognised body, if—

1.309Y.5.a

the function will require the person performing it to be involved in one or
more aspects of the body’s affairs, so far as relating to the activity, and

1.309Y.5.b

those aspects involve, or might involve, a risk of significant harm to the
body or to any of its consumers.

1.309Y.6

In this section, “ consumers ”, in relation to a relevant recognised body,
means—

1.309Y.6.a

persons who use, have used or may use a service provided by the body, or

1.309Y.6.b

persons who have relevant rights or interests in relation to any such service.

1.309Y.7

A person (“ P ”) has a “ relevant right or interest ” in relation to a service
provided by a relevant recognised body if P has a right or interest—

1.309Y.7.a

which is derived from, or is otherwise attributable to, the use of the service
by others, or

1.309Y.7.b

which may be adversely affected by the use of the service by persons acting on
P’s behalf or in a fiduciary capacity in relation to P.

1.309Y.8

For these purposes—

1.309Y.8.a

if a person is providing a service as a trustee, the persons who are, have
been or may be beneficiaries of the trust are to be treated as persons who
use, have used or may use the service;

1.309Y.8.b

a person who deals with another person (“ A ”) in the course of A providing a
service is to be treated as using the service.

########### Issuing certificates

1.309Z

1.309Z.1

A relevant recognised body may issue a certificate to a person under this
section in relation to a function only if the body is satisfied that the
person is a fit and proper person to perform the function.

1.309Z.2

In deciding that question the body must have regard, among other things, to
whether the person—

1.309Z.2.a

has obtained a specified qualification,

1.309Z.2.b

has undergone, or is undergoing, specified training,

1.309Z.2.c

possesses a specified level of competence, or

1.309Z.2.d

has specified personal characteristics.

1.309Z.3

In subsection  (2) , “ specified ” means specified in rules made by the
appropriate regulator.

1.309Z.4

A certificate issued by a relevant recognised body to a person under this
section must—

1.309Z.4.a

state that the body is satisfied that the person is a fit and proper person to
perform the function to which the certificate relates, and

1.309Z.4.b

set out the aspects of the body’s affairs in which the person will be involved
in performing the function.

1.309Z.5

A certificate issued under this section is valid for a period of 12 months
beginning with the day on which it is issued.

1.309Z.6

If, after having considered whether a person is a fit and proper person to
perform a function, a relevant recognised body decides not to issue a
certificate to the person under this section, the body must give the person a
notice in writing stating—

1.309Z.6.a

what steps (if any) the body proposes to take in relation to the person as a
result of the decision, and

1.309Z.6.b

the reasons for proposing to take those steps.

1.309Z.7

A relevant recognised body must maintain a record of every employee who has a
valid certificate issued by it under this section.

########## Rules of conduct

########### Rules of conduct

1.309Z1

1.309Z1.1

If it appears to the appropriate regulator to be necessary or expedient for
the purposes of advancing a relevant objective, the appropriate regulator may
make rules about the conduct of the following persons in relation to the
performance by them of qualifying functions—

1.309Z1.1.a

persons in relation to whom the appropriate regulator has given its approval
under section  309G  (“Part 18 approved persons”);

1.309Z1.1.b

directors of relevant recognised bodies;

1.309Z1.1.c

employees of relevant recognised bodies.

1.309Z1.2

Rules under subsection  (1)  may include provision requiring a relevant
recognised body to—

1.309Z1.2.a

notify persons mentioned in subsection  (1)  of the rules that apply to them;

1.309Z1.2.b

take specified steps to secure that such persons understand how those rules
apply in relation to them.

1.309Z1.3

Rules under subsection  (1)  may include provision requiring a relevant
recognised body to notify the appropriate regulator if the body takes
specified disciplinary action in relation to a person mentioned in subsection
(1) .

1.309Z1.4

In this section—

“ qualifying function ” means a function relating to the carrying on of
activities by the following— in the case of a Part 18 approved person, the
relevant recognised body on whose application approval was given; in the case
of a director or employee of a relevant recognised body, who is not a Part 18
approved person, the relevant recognised body; “ relevant objective ” means—
if the appropriate regulator is the FCA, any of its operational objectives; if
the appropriate regulator is the Bank of England, the Financial Stability
Objective. “ specified ” means specified in the rules.

########## Disciplinary action by appropriate regulator

########### Power to take disciplinary action for misconduct

1.309Z2

1.309Z2.1

Subsection  (2)  applies if—

1.309Z2.1.a

it appears to the appropriate regulator that a person is guilty of misconduct
(see section  309Z3 ), and

1.309Z2.1.b

the appropriate regulator is satisfied that it is appropriate in all the
circumstances to take action against the person.

1.309Z2.2

The appropriate regulator may do one or more of the following—

1.309Z2.2.a

publish a statement of the person’s misconduct;

1.309Z2.2.b

impose a penalty on the person of such amount as the appropriate regulator
considers appropriate;

1.309Z2.2.c

suspend an approval of the performance of a function by the person under
section  309G  for such period as the appropriate regulator considers
appropriate;

1.309Z2.2.d

impose such conditions as the appropriate regulator considers appropriate in
relation to such an approval for such period as the appropriate regulator
considers appropriate;

1.309Z2.2.e

limit the period for which such an approval is to have effect.

1.309Z2.3

Where the appropriate regulator takes action described in subsection  (2)(c) ,
(d)  or  (e) —

1.309Z2.3.a

it may not suspend an approval for more than 2 years;

1.309Z2.3.b

it may not impose conditions which have effect for more than 2 years;

1.309Z2.3.c

it may impose a condition so as to, among other things, require a person to
take, or refrain from taking, specified action;

1.309Z2.3.d

it may impose a suspension, condition or limitation that has effect in
relation to part of a function.

1.309Z2.4

The appropriate regulator that has taken action described in subsection
(2)(c) ,  (d)  or  (e)  may (at any time)—

1.309Z2.4.a

withdraw a suspension, condition or limitation;

1.309Z2.4.b

vary a suspension or condition so as to reduce the period for which it has
effect or otherwise to limit its effect;

1.309Z2.4.c

vary a limitation so as to increase the period for which the approval is to
have effect.

1.309Z2.5

The appropriate regulator may not take action under this section after the end
of the period of 6 years beginning with the first day on which the appropriate
regulator knew of the misconduct unless, before the end of that period, it
gave a warning notice to the person concerned under section  309Z4 .

1.309Z2.6

For the purposes of subsection  (5) , the appropriate regulator is to be
treated as knowing of misconduct if it has information from which the
misconduct can reasonably be inferred.

1.309Z2.7

When a suspension is in force under subsection  (2)(c)  in relation to part of
a function, the references in section  309G  and  309U  to the performance of
a function include the performance of part of a function.

1.309Z2.8

If at any time a condition imposed under subsection  (2)(d)  is contravened,
the approval in relation to the person concerned is to be treated for the
purposes of sections  309G  and  309U  as if it had been withdrawn at that
time.

########### Meaning of “misconduct”

1.309Z3

1.309Z3.1

For the purposes of section  309Z2 , a person is guilty of misconduct if any
of conditions A to C is met.

1.309Z3.2

Condition A is that—

1.309Z3.2.a

the person has at any time failed to comply with rules made under section
309Z1 , and

1.309Z3.2.b

at that time the person was—

1.309Z3.2.b.i

a Part 18 approved person,

1.309Z3.2.b.ii

an employee of a relevant recognised body, or

1.309Z3.2.b.iii

a director of a relevant recognised body.

1.309Z3.3

Condition B is that—

1.309Z3.3.a

the person has at any time after the passing of this Act been knowingly
concerned in a contravention by a relevant recognised body of a relevant
requirement, and

1.309Z3.3.b

at that time the person was—

1.309Z3.3.b.i

a Part 18 approved person in relation to the relevant recognised body,

1.309Z3.3.b.ii

an employee of the relevant recognised body, or

1.309Z3.3.b.iii

a director of the relevant recognised body.

1.309Z3.4

Condition C is that—

1.309Z3.4.a

the person has at any time been a Part 18 approved person in relation to a
relevant recognised body,

1.309Z3.4.b

at that time there was, or continued to be, a contravention by the body of a
relevant requirement,

1.309Z3.4.c

the person was at that time responsible for the management of any of the
body’s activities in relation to which the contravention occurred, and

1.309Z3.4.d

the person did not take such steps as a person in that position could
reasonably be expected to take to avoid the contravention occurring or
continuing.

1.309Z3.5

In this section—

“Part 18 approved person”— means a person in relation to whom an approval is
given under section  309G , and in relation to a relevant recognised body,
means a person in relation to whom such approval is given on the application
of the relevant recognised body; “ relevant requirement ” has the meaning
given by section 312E(2) and (3).

########### Procedure for disciplinary action

1.309Z4

1.309Z4.1

If the appropriate regulator proposes to take action against a person under
section  309Z2 , it must—

1.309Z4.1.a

give the person a warning notice, and

1.309Z4.1.b

in the case of proposed action under section  309Z2 (2)(c) ,  (d)  or  (e) ,
give each of the other interested parties a warning notice.

1.309Z4.2

A warning notice under this section about a proposal to publish a statement of
a person’s misconduct must set out the terms of the statement.

1.309Z4.3

A warning notice under this section about a proposal to impose a penalty must
state the amount of the penalty.

1.309Z4.4

A warning notice under this section about—

1.309Z4.4.a

a proposal to suspend an approval given under section  309G , or

1.309Z4.4.b

a proposal to impose a condition in relation to such an approval,

must state the period for which the suspension or condition is to have effect.

1.309Z4.5

A warning notice under this section about a proposal to limit the period for
which an approval under section  309G  is to have effect must state the length
of that period.

1.309Z4.6

If the appropriate regulator decides to take action against a person under
section  309Z2 , it must—

1.309Z4.6.a

give the person a decision notice, and

1.309Z4.6.b

in the case of proposed action under section  309Z2 (2)(c) ,  (d)  or  (e) ,
give each of the other interested parties a copy of the decision notice.

1.309Z4.7

A decision notice under this section about the publication of a statement of a
person’s misconduct must set out the terms of the statement.

1.309Z4.8

A decision notice under this section about the imposition of a penalty must
state the amount of the penalty.

1.309Z4.9

A decision notice under this section about—

1.309Z4.9.a

the suspension of an approval given under section  309G , or

1.309Z4.9.b

the imposition of a condition in relation to such an approval,

must state the period for which the suspension or condition is to have effect.

1.309Z4.10

A decision notice under this section about limiting the period for which an
approval under section  309G  is to have effect must state the length of that
period.

1.309Z4.11

If the appropriate regulator decides to take action against a person under
section  309Z2 —

1.309Z4.11.a

the person may refer the matter to the Tribunal, and

1.309Z4.11.b

in the case of proposed action under section  309Z2 (2)(c) ,  (d)  or  (e) ,
each of the other interested parties may also refer the matter to the
Tribunal.

1.309Z4.12

After a statement of a person’s misconduct is published under section  309Z2 ,
the appropriate regulator must send a copy of it to—

1.309Z4.12.a

the person concerned, and

1.309Z4.12.b

any person to whom a copy of the decision notice was given.

1.309Z4.13

In this section—

“ Part 18 approved person ”, in relation to a relevant recognised body, has
the meaning given by section  309Z3 (5) ; “ the other interested parties ”, in
relation to a Part 18 approved person in relation to a relevant recognised
body, are— the relevant recognised body, and the person by whom the Part 18
approved person’s services are retained, if different from the relevant
recognised body.

########### Statement of policy about disciplinary action

1.309Z5

1.309Z5.1

The appropriate regulator must prepare and issue a statement of its policy
with respect to—

1.309Z5.1.a

the imposition of penalties, suspensions, conditions or limitations under
section  309Z2 ,

1.309Z5.1.b

the amount of penalties under that section,

1.309Z5.1.c

the period for which suspensions or conditions under that section are to have
effect, and

1.309Z5.1.d

the period for which approvals under section  309G  are to have effect as a
result of a limitation under section  309Z2 .

1.309Z5.2

The appropriate regulator’s policy in determining what the amount of a penalty
should be, or what the period for which a suspension or restriction is to have
effect should be, must include having regard to—

1.309Z5.2.a

the seriousness of the misconduct in question,

1.309Z5.2.b

the extent to which that misconduct was deliberate or reckless, and

1.309Z5.2.c

whether the person against whom action is to be taken is an individual.

1.309Z5.3

The appropriate regulator—

1.309Z5.3.a

may alter or replace a statement issued under this section, and

1.309Z5.3.b

if it does so, must issue the altered or replacement statement.

1.309Z5.4

In exercising, or deciding whether to exercise, its power under section  309Z2
in the case of particular misconduct, the appropriate regulator must have
regard to any statement of policy published under this section and in force at
the time when the misconduct in question occurred.

########### Procedure for statement of policy about disciplinary action

1.309Z6

1.309Z6.1

Before the appropriate regulator issues a statement under section  309Z5 (1)
or  (3) , it must publish a draft of the proposed statement in the way
appearing to it to be best calculated to bring it to the attention of the
public.

1.309Z6.2

The draft statement must be accompanied by a notice stating that
representations about the proposal may be made to the appropriate regulator
within a period specified in the notice.

1.309Z6.3

Before issuing the proposed statement, the appropriate regulator must have
regard to any representations made to it in accordance with subsection  (2) .

1.309Z6.4

If the appropriate regulator issues the proposed statement it must publish the
following in the way appearing to the appropriate regulator to be best
calculated to bring it to the attention of the public—

1.309Z6.4.a

the statement,

1.309Z6.4.b

an account, in general terms, of the representations made to the appropriate
regulator in accordance with subsection  (2)  and the appropriate regulator’s
response to them, and

1.309Z6.4.c

if the statement differs from the draft published under subsection  (1)  in a
way which the appropriate regulator considers significant, details of the
difference.

1.309Z6.5

The appropriate regulator may charge a reasonable fee for providing a person
with—

1.309Z6.5.a

a copy of a draft statement published under subsection  (1) , or

1.309Z6.5.b

a copy of a statement published under subsection  (4)(a) .

1.309Z6.6

The appropriate regulator must, without delay, give the Treasury a copy of any
statement which it publishes under subsection  (4)(a) .

########## Interpretation

########### Interpretation of Chapter 2A

1.309Z7

1.309Z7.1

In this Chapter—

“ director ”, in relation to a relevant recognised body, means a member of the
board of directors of the body or, if there is no such board, the equivalent
body responsible for the management of the body; “ employee ”, in relation to
a relevant recognised body, includes a person who— personally provides, or is
under an obligation personally to provide, services to the body under an
arrangement made between the body and the person providing the services or
another person, and is subject to, or to the right of, supervision, direction
or control by the body as to the manner in which those services are provided;
“ relevant recognised body ” has the meaning given in section  309A ; “senior
management function” and “designated senior management function” have the
meanings given in section  309G  (see subsections  (3)  and  (5)  of that
section).

1.309Z7.2

In this Chapter, references to performing a designated senior management
function without approval have the meaning given in section  309U (3) .

########## Application of this Chapter to credit rating agencies

########### Power to apply this Chapter to credit rating agencies

1.309Z8

1.309Z8.1

The Treasury may by regulations provide for this Chapter, or any provision of
this Chapter, to apply (with or without modifications) in relation to—

1.309Z8.1.a

registered credit rating agencies, or

1.309Z8.1.b

registered credit rating agencies of descriptions specified in the
regulations.

1.309Z8.2

Regulations under subsection  (1)  must provide for the FCA to be the
appropriate regulator in relation to a registered credit rating agency to
which any provision of this Chapter is applied by the regulations.

1.309Z8.3

Regulations under subsection  (1)  may modify legislation (including any
provision of, or made under, this Act).

1.309Z8.4

Before making regulations under subsection  (1) , the Treasury must consult—

1.309Z8.4.a

the FCA, and

1.309Z8.4.b

such other persons who appear to the Treasury to be representative of persons
likely to be affected by the application of this Chapter to registered credit
rating agencies, or registered credit rating agencies of descriptions
specified in the regulations.

1.309Z8.5

In this section—

“ legislation ” means primary legislation, subordinate legislation (within the
meaning of the Interpretation Act 1978) and retained direct EU legislation,
but does not include rules or other instruments made by any regulator; “
modify ” includes amend, repeal or revoke; “ registered credit rating agency ”
means a credit rating agency registered in accordance with Regulation  (EC) No
1060/2009  of the European Parliament and the Council of 16 September 2009 on
credit rating agencies.

  Central counterparties

Section 57

##### Introductory

###### Overview

1

1.1

The purpose of the special resolution regime for CCPs (see Part 5 of this
Schedule) is to address the situation where all or part of the business of a
CCP has encountered, or is likely to encounter, financial difficulties.

1.2

The special resolution regime consists of the eight stabilisation options.

1.3

The eight stabilisation options are—

1.3.a

transfer to a private sector purchaser (paragraph  27 ),

1.3.b

transfer to a bridge central counterparty (paragraph  29 ),

1.3.c

transfer of ownership (paragraph  30 ),

1.3.d

terminating clearing member contracts (paragraph  31 ),

1.3.e

making a cash call (paragraph  32 ),

1.3.f

reducing variation margin payments (paragraph  33 ),

1.3.g

writing down liabilities (paragraphs  34  and  35 ), and

1.3.h

taking control of the CCP (paragraph  38 ).

1.4

The stabilisation options are achieved through the exercise of one or more of
the “stabilisation powers” which are—

1.4.a

the share transfer powers (paragraphs  41  and  49  to  53 ),

1.4.b

the property transfer powers (paragraphs  54  and  67  to  74 ), and

1.4.c

the other resolution powers (paragraphs  31  to  35  and  38 ).

1.5

Each of the following has a role in the operation of the special resolution
regime—

1.5.a

the Bank,

1.5.b

the Treasury,

1.5.c

the PRA, and

1.5.d

the FCA.

1.6

Other Parts of this Schedule deal with the following matters—

1.6.a

powers and requirements in relation to CCPs which are exercisable by the Bank
in advance of reliance on the special resolution regime (see Parts 2 to 4);

1.6.b

powers relating to information, investigation and enforcement in relation to
requirements under this Schedule (see Part 6);

1.6.c

third-country resolution action (see Part 7);

1.6.d

other general provision, financial provision and consequential amendments (see
Parts 8 to 10).

##### Pre-resolution powers of the Bank of England

###### Removal of impediments to the exercise of stabilisation powers etc

2

2.1

The Bank may give directions to a CCP to take measures which the Bank
considers are required to address impediments to the effective exercise of the
stabilisation powers.

2.2

The power conferred by sub-paragraph  (1)  includes (but is not limited to) a
power to direct the CCP—

2.2.a

to enter into or revise an agreement for the provision of services relating to
the provision of critical clearing services;

2.2.b

to limit its maximum individual and aggregate exposures to loss;

2.2.c

to produce information which is relevant to the exercise of the stabilisation
powers, and to provide that information to the Bank;

2.2.d

to dispose of specified assets;

2.2.e

to cease carrying out specified activities, or observe restrictions in
relation to the carrying out of specified activities;

2.2.f

to cease the development of new or existing business operations, or observe
restrictions in relation to the development of such operations;

2.2.g

to make specified changes to its recovery plan, rules or contractual
arrangements;

2.2.h

in order to ensure that it is possible for the performance of critical
clearing services to be legally or operationally separated from the
performance of other functions—

2.2.h.i

to change its legal or operational structure, or

2.2.h.ii

so far as it is able to do so, to change the legal or operational structure of
a subsidiary;

2.2.i

to change its operational and financial arrangements so as to separate
specified classes of assets from other specified classes of assets;

2.2.j

to restrict netting sets in relation to specified classes of assets;

2.2.k

to establish a parent company in the United Kingdom.

2.3

Where a CCP is a subsidiary of a company incorporated in the United Kingdom,
the Bank may give directions to its parent company requiring the parent
company to establish a separate holding company as a parent of the subsidiary
for the purpose of—

2.3.a

facilitating the exercise of the stabilisation powers, or

2.3.b

ensuring that the exercise of a stabilisation power does not have an adverse
effect on any other entities in the group.

2.4

Before giving directions under this paragraph the Bank must have regard to the
potential impact of the direction on—

2.4.a

the CCP or entity in question,

2.4.b

the market for financial services within the United Kingdom, and

2.4.c

the financial stability of the United Kingdom.

2.5

Where the CCP in question is a PRA-authorised person, the Bank must consult
the PRA before giving directions under this paragraph.

2.6

Directions under this paragraph—

2.6.a

must be in writing,

2.6.b

may be given with general effect or with respect to a particular CCP or class
of CCPs, and

2.6.c

may be varied or revoked.

2.7

Nothing in this paragraph limits the powers of the Bank under section 296 or
296A of, or paragraph 9B of Schedule 17A to, FSMA 2000.

2.8

In this paragraph, “ recovery plan ” in relation to a CCP, means a plan
required under paragraph 29B of the Schedule to the Financial Services and
Markets Act 2000 (Recognition Requirements for Investment Exchanges, Clearing
Houses and Central Securities Depositories) Regulations 2001 ( S.I. 2001/995
).

###### Safeguards relating to directions under paragraph 

3

3.1

A direction given to a relevant person under paragraph  2  must be accompanied
by a notice which—

3.1.a

states when the direction takes effect (see sub-paragraphs  (2)  and  (3) ),

3.1.b

gives the Bank’s reasons for giving the direction, and

3.1.c

specifies a reasonable period within which the person may make representations
to the Bank about the direction.

3.2

The direction may, if the Bank considers it necessary, take effect—

3.2.a

immediately it is given to the relevant person, or

3.2.b

on a later date specified in the direction.

3.3

In any other case the direction takes effect when—

3.3.a

it has been confirmed by a notice under sub-paragraph  (5) , and

3.3.b

the period during which the direction may be referred to the Upper Tribunal
(under sub-paragraph  (6) ) has expired and, if the matter was so referred,
the reference and any appeal against the Tribunal’s determination, has been
finally disposed of.

3.4

Where representations are made by the relevant person within the period
specified under sub-paragraph  (1)(c) , the Bank must, within a reasonable
period, consider those representations and decide—

3.4.a

whether to confirm or revoke the direction, and

3.4.b

if the direction is revoked, whether to give a different direction.

3.5

The Bank must—

3.5.a

if no representations are made within that specified period, give the relevant
person written notice that the direction is confirmed, and

3.5.b

if representations are made, give the relevant person written notice of its
decision under sub-paragraph  (4) .

3.6

If the relevant person is aggrieved by the confirmation of the direction, the
person may refer the matter to the Upper Tribunal.

3.7

A notice under sub-paragraph  (5)(a)  or  (b)  confirming the direction must—

3.7.a

inform the relevant person of the right to refer the matter to the Upper
Tribunal, and

3.7.b

indicate the procedure on such a reference.

3.8

A notice given under sub-paragraph  (5)(b)  of a decision by the Bank to give
a different direction must comply with sub-paragraph  (1) .

3.9

The Bank must prepare and publish a statement of its policy with respect to
the giving of directions under paragraph  2 .

3.10

The Bank may alter or replace a statement of policy published under this
paragraph.

3.11

The Bank must publish a statement as altered or replaced under sub-paragraph
(10) .

3.12

No directions may be given under paragraph  2  before the statement of policy
under sub-paragraph  (9)  has been published.

3.13

In this paragraph “ relevant person ” means—

3.13.a

a CCP, or

3.13.b

a parent of a CCP.

##### Resolution plans

###### Resolution plans

4

4.1

The Treasury may by regulations make provision requiring the Bank to create
and maintain a resolution plan for each CCP.

4.2

The following are examples of provision that regulations under sub-paragraph
(1)  may make—

4.2.a

provision specifying the information that must be contained in a resolution
plan (including provision enabling the Bank to specify such information);

4.2.b

provision requiring CCPs to give specified information to the Bank for the
purpose of the Bank creating and maintaining a resolution plan (including
provision enabling the Bank to specify the way in which such information is to
be given);

4.2.c

provision specifying the form of resolution plans (including provision
enabling the Bank to specify the form);

4.2.d

provision requiring the Bank to review resolution plans at specified
intervals;

4.2.e

provision requiring the Bank to provide specified information relating to a
review to specified persons;

4.2.f

provision requiring the Bank to give specified persons a copy of the
resolution plan and any revised plans (including provision about the way in
which a copy of a plan is to be given).

4.3

Regulations under this paragraph may provide for exemptions.

4.4

Regulations under this paragraph are subject to the negative procedure.

4.5

In this paragraph “ resolution plan ”, in relation to a CCP, means a document
setting out the actions that the Bank proposes to take in the event that the
CCP meets the conditions under paragraph  17  for the exercise of the
stabilisation powers.

##### Removal of directors and senior managers

###### Removal of directors and senior managers

5

5.1

If the Bank is satisfied that the conditions in paragraph  7 (1) and (2) are
met in relation to a CCP, the Bank may require the CCP to remove—

5.1.a

any person who is a director of the CCP;

5.1.b

any person who is a senior manager of the CCP.

5.2

If the Bank imposes a requirement under sub-paragraph  (1) , the Bank may also
require the CCP—

5.2.a

to replace a director or senior manager who has been removed, and

5.2.b

to take any step needed to give effect to the replacement, including, where
necessary, calling a general meeting of the CCP’s shareholders or, if the CCP
is an unincorporated association, its members.

5.3

If the Bank is satisfied that the condition in paragraph  7(5)  is met in
relation to a person who is a director of a CCP, the Bank may require that CCP
to remove that person from the board of directors.

5.4

Nothing in this Schedule affects the powers under Article 31 of EMIR or
paragraphs  45  and  58 .

###### Temporary manager

6

6.1

If the Bank is satisfied that the conditions in paragraph  7 (1), (2) and (4)
are met in relation to a CCP, the Bank may appoint a person to act (or more
than one persons to act jointly) as a temporary manager of that CCP.

6.2

A temporary manager may be appointed under sub-paragraph  (1) —

6.2.a

to replace the directors of a CCP where they have been removed in compliance
with a requirement imposed under paragraph  5 , or

6.2.b

to work with the directors of a CCP.

6.3

A temporary manager has the functions specified in the instrument of
appointment (see paragraph  9 ).

6.4

The functions which may be specified include (amongst other things)—

6.4.a

ascertaining the financial position of the CCP;

6.4.b

managing the business or part of the business of the CCP in order to preserve
or restore the financial position of the CCP;

6.4.c

taking measures to restore the prudent management of the CCP;

6.4.d

any functions of the directors.

6.5

The temporary manager may, with the consent of the Bank—

6.5.a

require the directors to call a general meeting of the shareholders, or in the
case of an unincorporated association, the members of the CCP, or

6.5.b

in the case where all of the directors have been removed in compliance with a
requirement imposed under paragraph  5 , call a general meeting of the
shareholders of the CCP or, if the CCP is an unincorporated association, the
members of the CCP.

6.6

The temporary manager may propose business for consideration at the general
meeting.

6.7

If the temporary manager is being appointed to work with the directors, the
Bank—

6.7.a

may require the directors not to exercise specified functions during the
period of appointment;

6.7.b

may require the directors to consult the temporary manager, or obtain the
consent of the temporary manager, before taking such decisions or actions as
may be specified in the requirement.

###### Paragraphs 

7

7.1

The condition in this sub-paragraph is met if—

7.1.a

there is a significant deterioration in the financial situation of the CCP, or

7.1.b

there is a serious infringement by the CCP of—

7.1.b.i

a relevant requirement, or

7.1.b.ii

its rules.

7.2

The condition in this sub-paragraph is met if it is not reasonably likely that
the deterioration would be reversed or the infringement would be brought to an
end by any measure which could be taken by the Bank under the provisions
listed in sub-paragraph  (3) .

7.3

The provisions mentioned in sub-paragraph  (2)  are—

7.3.a

section 296 or 296A of FSMA 2000 (power to direct CCPs);

7.3.b

paragraph  13  (power to impose stay on distributions).

7.4

The condition in this sub-paragraph is met if the imposition of one or more
requirements under paragraph  5  (removal and replacement of directors and
senior managers) would not be sufficient to reverse the deterioration or bring
the infringement to an end.

7.5

The condition in this sub-paragraph is met in relation to a director of a CCP,
if the director—

7.5.a

is no longer of sufficiently good repute to perform their duties,

7.5.b

no longer possesses sufficient knowledge, skills, experience, honesty,
integrity or independence of mind to perform their duties, or

7.5.c

is no longer able to commit sufficient time to perform their duties.

7.6

For the purposes of this paragraph—

7.6.a

“ relevant requirement ” means a requirement imposed by or under—

7.6.a.i

FSMA 2000;

7.6.a.ii

EMIR;

7.6.a.iii

another enactment (or provision of an enactment) specified in regulations made
by the Treasury;

7.6.b

a deterioration in the financial situation of a CCP is significant if the
deterioration places the CCP at risk of meeting condition 1 under paragraph
17 .

7.7

Regulations under this paragraph are subject to the negative procedure.

###### Temporary manager: further provisions in relation to the appointment

8

8.1

Before appointing a person to act as a temporary manager, the Bank must be
satisfied that the person—

8.1.a

has the qualifications, ability and knowledge to carry out the functions to be
given to the temporary manager, and

8.1.b

would not be subject to a conflict of interest as a result of the appointment.

8.2

A person may not be appointed to act as a temporary manager for a period
longer than one year, but is eligible for re-appointment (or further re-
appointment) if paragraph  6 (1) continues to apply in relation to the CCP.

8.3

The Bank may vary the terms of the appointment of a temporary manager, or
remove the temporary manager, at any time.

8.4

A temporary manager is not liable for damages in respect of anything done in
good faith for the purposes of or in connection with the functions of the
appointment (subject to section 8 of the Human Rights Act 1998).

###### Temporary manager: instrument of appointment

9

9.1

The power in paragraph 6(1) is to be exercised by an instrument of
appointment.

9.2

The instrument of appointment must—

9.2.a

specify the functions of the temporary manager,

9.2.b

specify the date on which the appointment of the temporary manager has effect,

9.2.c

specify the period for which the temporary manager is appointed, and

9.2.d

make provision for the resignation and replacement of the person who is
appointed as the temporary manager.

9.3

The instrument of appointment may—

9.3.a

require the temporary manager to consult the Bank or other specified person
before exercising specified functions,

9.3.b

specify particular matters on which the Bank or other specified person must be
consulted, and

9.3.c

provide that the temporary manager is not to exercise specified functions
without the consent of the Bank or other specified person.

9.4

The instrument of appointment may require the temporary manager to make
reports to the Bank, at specified times or intervals, on—

9.4.a

the financial position of the CCP,

9.4.b

the actions taken by the temporary manager during the course of the temporary
manager‘s appointment, and

9.4.c

any other specified matters.

9.5

The instrument of appointment may provide for the payment of remuneration and
allowances to a temporary manager.

9.6

Provision under sub-paragraph  (5)  may provide that the amounts are—

9.6.a

to be paid by the Bank, or

9.6.b

to be determined by the Bank and paid by the CCP.

9.7

If a temporary manager—

9.7.a

is appointed to replace the directors of the CCP, or

9.7.b

is appointed to work with the directors of the CCP and has the power to
represent the CCP,

the Bank must publish the instrument of appointment on its website.

###### Right to refer matters to the Tribunal

10

10.1

A CCP which is aggrieved by one of the following may refer the matter to the
Tribunal—

10.1.a

the imposition of a requirement on that CCP under paragraph  5 , or

10.1.b

the appointment, or the terms of the appointment, of a person to act as a
temporary manager of that CCP under paragraph  6 .

10.2

A director or senior manager (or a former director or senior manager) of a CCP
who is aggrieved by the imposition of a requirement on that CCP under
paragraph  5  may refer the matter to the Tribunal.

10.3

A director (or a former director) of a CCP who is aggrieved by the imposition
of a requirement on that director under paragraph  6(7)  may refer the matter
to the Tribunal.

###### Removal of directors and senior managers and appointment of temporary manager: procedure

11

11.1

A requirement under paragraph  5  or  6(7)  or the appointment of a temporary
manager under paragraph  6(1)  may be expressed to take effect immediately or
on a specified date only if the Bank, having regard to the grounds for
imposing the requirement or making the appointment, reasonably considers that
it is necessary for the requirement or the appointment to take effect
immediately or on that date.

11.2

If the Bank proposes to impose a requirement on a CCP under paragraph  5  or
imposes such a requirement with immediate effect, it must give written notice—

11.2.a

to that CCP, and

11.2.b

to each of the directors or senior managers to whom the requirement relates.

11.3

If the Bank—

11.3.a

proposes to appoint a person to act as a temporary manager under paragraph  6
or to vary the terms on which such a person is appointed, or

11.3.b

makes such an appointment or variation with immediate effect,

the Bank must give written notice to the CCP.

11.4

If the Bank proposes to impose a requirement on the directors under paragraph
6(7) , or imposes such a requirement with immediate effect, the Bank must give
written notice to each director.

11.5

If, having considered any representations made by a person to whom notice (the
“original notice”) has been given (see paragraph  12 ), the Bank decides—

11.5.a

to impose the requirement, make the appointment or vary the terms of an
appointment in accordance with the original notice, or

11.5.b

not to rescind the imposition of any such requirement or the making of any
such appointment or variation which has already taken effect,

the Bank must give written notice to each person to whom the original notice
was given.

11.6

A written notice under sub-paragraph  (5)  must inform the person to whom it
is given of the right of that person to refer the matter to the Tribunal and
give an indication of the procedure on such a reference.

11.7

If, having considered any representations made by a person to whom the
original notice has been given (see paragraph  12 ), the Bank decides—

11.7.a

to impose a requirement, make an appointment or vary the terms of an
appointment in a way that is different from the requirement, appointment or
variation described in the original notice,

11.7.b

not to impose the requirement, make the appointment or vary the terms of an
appointment in accordance with the original notice, or

11.7.c

to rescind the imposition of any such requirement, or the making of any such
appointment or variation that has already taken effect,

the Bank must give written notice to each person to whom the original notice
was given.

###### Removal of directors and senior managers and appointment of temporary manager: notice requirements

12

12.1

A notice under paragraph  11(2)  must—

12.1.a

give details of the requirement,

12.1.b

identify each of the directors or senior managers to whom the requirement
relates (“the interested parties”),

12.1.c

give the Bank’s reasons for imposing the requirement—

12.1.c.i

in the case of a notice given to the CCP, in relation to each interested
party;

12.1.c.ii

in the case of a notice given to an interested party, in relation to that
interested party,

12.1.d

inform the CCP and the interested parties that each of them may make
representations to the Bank within such period as may be specified in the
notice (whether or not the matter has been referred to the Tribunal),

12.1.e

state when the requirement takes effect, and

12.1.f

inform the CCP and each of the interested parties of their right to refer the
matter to the Tribunal.

12.2

A notice given under paragraph  11(3)  must—

12.2.a

state when the appointment or variation takes effect, and be accompanied by
the instrument, or revised instrument, of appointment,

12.2.b

give the Bank’s reasons for making the appointment or variation,

12.2.c

inform the CCP that it may make representations to the Bank within such period
as may be specified in the notice (whether or not the matter has been referred
to the Tribunal), and

12.2.d
